        - How to read non-fiction books:

1. Read first 30%
2. Stop &amp; save highlights to a digital notes app
3. Add summary of how/when you think this material would be most useful
4. Search these notes next time you start a project 
5. Finish reading books most likely to be useful

        - New acronym for every place I have to review or clear during my Weekly Review:

ECIDNOWT

            - https://twitter.com/fortelabs/status/1170851038599012353

        - Originally, oral dictation was considered just as much a part of word processing as full screen text editing.         - Word processing as a practice and a concept rode the wave of the ‚Äúpaperwork explosion‚Äù that executives faced, which was the earliest incarnation of the more general info explosion. WP both addressed the need to process more paperwork, and also contributed to it https://t.co/dfjtCQfzIE
            - https://twitter.com/fortelabs/status/1170831074492059651
